FLASHCARD REQUIREMENTS
- minimum 12 flashcards per deck
- at least 100 flashcards total across all decks
- each card must have concise front and back
- no filler
- no repeated cards
- no vague wording

FLASHCARD STYLE
Front:
- term, abbreviation, formula, drug, or concept

Back:
- concise explanation or correct expansion
- useful for memorization
- no long paragraph answers

EXAMPLES OF GOOD FLASHCARD STYLES
- “bid” → “Twice daily”
- “C-II” → “Schedule II controlled substance with high abuse potential and accepted medical use”
- “Amoxicillin” → “Generic antibiotic in the penicillin class”
- “mL per dose formula” → “Desired dose ÷ dose on hand × quantity”

ROUTE

- update skill estimate
- adjust next question difficulty

Session length options:
10 questions
25 questions
50 questions
unlimited adaptive practice

==================================================
QUESTION DIFFICULTY TIERS
==================================================

easy
medium
hard

RULES

Correct answer:

medium → next medium or hard

hard → remain hard or medium

Incorrect answer:

hard → drop to medium

medium → drop to easy

easy → remain easy

pharmacy law

workflow

prioritize questions from that category.

==================================================

1. difficulty
2. category accuracy
3. recent question history
4. user mastery score

Do not repeat the same question within a session.

Prefer unseen questions first.

Build a personalized Pharmacy Technician study plan generator for NurseNest Allied.

PRIMARY GOAL
Create a student-facing study planner that automatically builds a structured study schedule based on exam date, available study time, weak areas, and current mastery levels.

This planner must integrate with:
- Pharmacy Technician lessons
- flashcard decks
- practice questions
- adaptive practice
- mock exams
- weak-area recommendations
- mastery tracking

ROUTES TO CREATE
- /allied/pharmacy-technician/study-plan
- /allied/pharmacy-technician/study-plan/:planId
- /admin/allied-content/pharmacy-technician/study-plans

CORE USE CASE
A learner enters:
- target exam date
- days per week available
- minutes or hours per study session
- whether they want light, balanced, or intensive pace
- optional weak areas or confidence ratings
- optional preference for flashcards vs questions vs lessons

The system generates:
- a multi-week study schedule
- weekly goals
- daily tasks
- topic sequence
- review blocks
- exam checkpoints
- final revision phase

DATABASE TABLES

Create:
pharmtech_study_plans
- id
- user_id
- title
- exam_date
- start_date
- pace
- days_per_week
- minutes_per_session
- preferred_content_mix_json
- weak_areas_json
- mastery_snapshot_json
- generated_plan_json
- status
- created_at
- updated_at

pharmtech_study_plan_tasks
- id
- plan_id
- week_number
- day_number
- task_type
- task_title
- task_description
- linked_route
- linked_content_type
- linked_content_id
- estimated_minutes
- category
- is_completed
- created_at
- updated_at

STUDY PLAN INPUT FORM
Build a form that collects:
- exam date
- available study days per week
- average minutes per study session
- pace:
  - light
  - balanced
  - intensive
- preferred learning style:
  - more flashcards
  - more practice questions
  - more lessons
  - mixed
- optional weak areas:
  - pharmacy law
  - medication safety
  - dosage calculations
  - drug classes
  - top 200 drugs
  - sig codes
  - compounding
  - inventory
  - workflow
- optional checkbox:
  - use my adaptive practice results

PLAN GENERATION LOGIC

General rules:
- start with foundations if no mastery data exists
- if mastery data exists, prioritize weak categories first
- schedule a mix of:
  - lessons
  - flashcards
  - short quizzes
  - adaptive practice
  - mock exams
- include repetition and review
- include spaced review blocks
- include a final exam-prep phase before the exam date

PACE RULES

Light pace:
- fewer tasks per week
- more review spacing
- more manageable sessions

Balanced pace:
- standard workload
- steady mix of lessons, flashcards, and questions

Intensive pace:
- more frequent tasks
- more practice questions
- more mock exams
- shorter interval between review cycles

PLAN STRUCTURE

Each plan should include:
1. Foundation phase
2. Core category phase
3. Weak-area reinforcement phase
4. Mock exam phase
5. Final review phase

If the exam date is close:
- compress schedule
- prioritize high-yield content
- reduce low-priority extras

TASK TYPES TO SCHEDULE
- lesson study
- flashcard deck study
- 10-question quiz
- 25-question quiz
- adaptive practice session
- mock exam
- review weak areas
- final revision session

CATEGORY PRIORITY RULES
If no user data:
Prioritize in this order:
1. foundations
2. law and ethics
3. medication safety
4. sig codes
5. dosage calculations
6. drug classes
7. top 200 drugs
8. compounding
9. inventory
10. controlled substances

If user has adaptive data:
Prioritize lowest mastery categories first.

MASTERY-BASED RULES
Use mastery levels if available:
- Beginner: prioritize heavily
- Developing: schedule regular reinforcement
- Proficient: maintain with lighter review
- Advanced: occasional mixed review only

TASK LINKING
Every generated task should link directly to the appropriate content:
- lesson pages
- flashcard decks
- quizzes
- exams
- adaptive practice

STUDENT VIEW
Create a study plan page that shows:
- overview card
- exam date countdown
- study pace
- weekly schedule
- daily tasks
- completion checkboxes
- progress bar
- weak areas being targeted
- recommended next task

WEEKLY LAYOUT
Show:
Week 1
- Day 1: lesson
- Day 2: flashcards
- Day 3: quiz
- Day 4: lesson + flashcards
- Day 5: adaptive review

Allow:
- mark complete
- open linked task
- reschedule unfinished tasks

RESCHEDULING LOGIC
If a task is missed:
- allow move to another day
- or auto-roll unfinished tasks forward if enabled

PROGRESS TRACKING
Track:
- completed tasks
- remaining tasks
- completion percent
- categories covered
- mock exams completed
- improving mastery areas

RECOMMENDATION SYSTEM
As the user completes tasks:
- recommend next lesson
- recommend next quiz
- recommend flashcard refresh
- recommend mock exam when enough categories are covered

INTEGRATION WITH ADAPTIVE PRACTICE
If adaptive data exists:
- use weak categories to shape the plan
- update recommendations as mastery changes
- allow “refresh my study plan” to regenerate the later weeks

PLAN TYPES TO SUPPORT

- 12-week comprehensive plan

PRESET PLAN OPTIONS

- 2-week crash plan

- 8-week mastery plan

- supportive

- clean
- not cluttered

- soft rounded cards

SEO / PAGE COPY

- SEO title

  - no rationale visible
  - no “show explanation” button
  - no correct answer explanation after item submission
  - no answer teaching popups
- Practice mode:
  - rationale visible after submission
  - correct answer shown after submission
  - optional remediation box allowed

EXAMPLE LOGIC:

const shouldShowRationale =
  examMode === "practice" &&
  questionSubmitted === true &&
  !!question.rationale;

const shouldShowCorrectAnswer =
  examMode === "practice" &&
  questionSubmitted === true;

if (examMode === "cat") {
  hide rationale;
  hide correct answer explanation;
}

IMPORTANT:
- Preserve accessibility.
- Preserve current NurseNest brand styling.
- Do not break adaptive scoring.
- Do not accidentally expose rationale through collapsed accordions, tooltips, hidden divs, or console logs.
- Prevent rationale from being rendered at all in CAT mode, not just visually hidden with CSS.

AFTER IMPLEMENTATION:
- Test CAT mode with a Pharmacy Technician exam.
- Test Practice mode with the same questions.
- Confirm rationale displays only in Practice mode.
- Confirm adaptive engine still works.

TASK: Create a validation layer for NurseNest question bank imports so unrealistic, broken, duplicate, vague, or low-quality Pharmacy Technician questions do not get added to the exam pool.

GOAL:
Every imported question must pass structural validation and quality validation before it can enter the live exam bank.

STRUCTURAL VALIDATION RULES:
- id required
- question required
- options required
- exactly 4 options required unless future question type allows otherwise
- correct_answer required
- rationale required
- exam_tier required
- exam_type required
- category required
- difficulty required
- correct_answer must match one of the option keys
- no duplicate ids
- no blank option text

QUALITY VALIDATION RULES:
- question must be clear and grammatically correct
- one best answer only
- no trick wording unless pedagogically justified
- no obviously outdated law wording without jurisdiction tagging
- no nonsensical distractors
- no duplicate answer options
- no answer giveaways such as longest option always being correct
- rationale must explain why the correct answer is correct
- rationale should be concise but educational
- difficulty must match the actual complexity
- category must fit the content
- do not allow mixed professions like RN-only clinical judgment questions into pharmtech bank

PHARMACY TECHNICIAN SPECIFIC CONTENT GUARDRAILS:
- prioritize pharmacy workflow, calculations, law, safety, dispensing, sterile compounding, nonsterile compounding, pharmacology basics, medication storage, controlled substances, abbreviations, and technician scope
- avoid physician-only diagnostic reasoning
- avoid advanced RN bedside priority framing unless clearly adapted to pharmacy technician scope

OUTPUT REQUIREMENTS:
- For each failed question, show:
  - id
  - pass/fail
  - errors
  - warnings
  - suggested correction
- Allow admin to fix and resubmit

IMPORTANT:
- Do not auto-publish failed questions
- Do not silently modify content without showing the changes
- Keep the validator reusable across all NurseNest tiers

Test all of the following before considering implementation complete.

EXAMS
- Pharm Tech CAT pulls only Pharm Tech CAT questions
- rationale hidden in CAT mode
- rationale visible in Practice mode
- no cross-tier question leakage
- adaptive difficulty changes
- category performance stored

LESSONS
- lesson pages load correctly
- Pharm Tech lessons only show in Pharm Tech section
- SEO metadata renders correctly
- published lessons appear live
- draft lessons do not appear publicly

FLASHCARDS
- Pharm Tech decks filter correctly
- cards render properly
- deck pages work on mobile
- related lesson linking works

ADMIN
- bulk exam import works
- bulk lesson import works
- bulk flashcard import works
- validation catches malformed entries
- publish toggle works
- live site reflects published content

======================================================================
PART 17: DO NOT DO THESE THINGS
======================================================================

- Do not mix Pharm Tech content with other tiers
- Do not move Pharm Tech lessons into free tier by default
- Do not expose rationale in CAT mode
- Do not save published content only inside Replit workspace memory
- Do not create ugly generic admin pages with no filtering
- Do not make childish exam visuals
- Do not create thin SEO pages with almost no content
- Do not break existing NurseNest architecture
- Do not hardcode everything in a way that prevents scaling to other professions later
